ltm rule /Common/HTTP-TO-HTTPS-WWW {

ltm rule /Common/honeypot-ftp {
when RULE_INIT {
  set static::DEBUG 0
  set static::sec_block_ftp 1
  set name "none"  
}

when CLIENT_ACCEPTED {
  if { $static::DEBUG } { log local0. "Client Accepted" }
  TCP::respond "220 Microsoft FTP Service\r\n";
  TCP::collect
  #TCP::release  
}

when CLIENT_DATA {
  if { $static::DEBUG } { log local0. "----------------------------------------------------------" }
  if { $static::DEBUG } { log local0. "LOG:payload [TCP::payload]" }
  set client_data [string trim [TCP::payload]]
  set cmd [string toupper [lindex [split $client_data " "] 0]]
  set value  [lindex [split $client_data " "] 1]  
  switch $cmd {
    "USER" {
        set name $value
        if { $static::DEBUG } { 
                log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:FTPHoneypot login attempt detected as $name"
        }
        if { $static::sec_block_ftp } {
                TCP::respond "331 Password ******
        }
    }
    "PASS" {
        if { $static::DEBUG } { log local0. "LOG:Password ******
        if { $static::sec_block_ftp } {
                TCP::respond "530 User $name cannot log in.\r\n";
                log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], USERNAME: $name, VIP:[virtual name], MESG:FTP Honeypot Attack"
        }
    }
        "QUIT" {
                TCP::respond "221  \r\n"
                TCP::close
    }
        "SYST" {
                TCP::respond "530 Please login with USER and PASS.\r\n";
    }
  }
  TCP::payload replace 0 [string length [TCP::payload]] ""
  #TCP::release  
  TCP::collect  
}

when CLIENT_CLOSED {
  if { $static::DEBUG } { 
        log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Client Closed"
  }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/honeypot-http {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
        if { [TCP::local_port] equals 80 and [HTTP::uri] equals "/" } {
                HTTP::redirect "http://www.factset.com"
                log local0.info "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:HTTP Honeypot 302"
        } else {
                HTTP::respond 200 "Connection" "close" "Blocked" "true"
                log local0.info "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:HTTP Honeypot 200"
                TCP::close
        }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-block-500 {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
  set HTTP_URI [HTTP::uri]
  set HTTP_HOST [HTTP::host]
}

when HTTP_RESPONSE {
if { [HTTP::status] starts_with 50} {
     set client_ip [IP::client_addr]
     log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:$HTTP_HOST, URI:$HTTP_URI, VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Blocked URI with HTTP Status [HTTP::status]"
     HTTP::redirect "http://www.factset.com/files/landingpages/maintenance.html"
    } 
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-blockhiddencontent {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    if {[HTTP::uri] matches_regex {\/\.(?!well-known\/)}} {
        log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Contains Dot"
        HTTP::respond 200 "Connection" "close" "Blocked" "true"
        TCP::close
    }

    switch -glob [string tolower [HTTP::uri]] {
        *cmd.exe* -
        *telnet.exe* -
        *root.exe* -
        *ping.exe* -
        *awstats.pl?* {
        log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Contains some .exe"
        HTTP::respond 405
        discard
        }
    }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-callstreet-audiotoken {
when RULE_INIT {
   # Log debug messages to /var/log/ltm?  1=yes, 0=no.
   set static::audiotoken_http_debug 0
}



when HTTP_REQUEST timing on {

set HTTP_URI [HTTP::uri]
set HTTP_HOST [HTTP::host]
set uri_request [HTTP::uri]
set Filename [URI::basename $uri_request]
set client_hash [URI::query $uri_request auth]

set datenow [clock scan now]
set day_of_year_str [clock format $datenow -format %j]
scan $day_of_year_str "%d" day_of_year_int
set year [clock format  $datenow -format %Y]
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug}  {log local0. "day_of_year $day_of_year_int"}
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0. "year $year" }



set bigip_client_ip  [IP::client_addr]
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:$HTTP_HOST, URI:$HTTP_URI, VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Sent hash"}
set temp "$day_of_year_int$year,$Filename,$bigip_client_ip,secret"

if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0. "Building hash from $temp"}

set temp1 [b64encode $temp]
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug}  {log local0. "b64encoded $temp1"}
set bigip_hash [b64encode [md5 $temp1]]
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0. "bigip_hash $bigip_hash"}
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:$HTTP_HOST, URI:$HTTP_URI, VIP:[virtual name], MESG:candidate hash1: $temp -> $bigip_hash"}
set day_of_year_min_one {expr $day_of_year_int-1}
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug}  {log local0. "day_of_year_min_one $day_of_year_min_one"}
set temp "$day_of_year_min_one$year,$Filename,$bigip_client_ip,secret"

if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug}  {log local0. "constructed string2 $temp"}

set temp1 [b64encode $temp]
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug}  {log local0. "b64encoded $temp1"}
set bigip_hash2 [b64encode [md5 $temp1]]
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug}  {log local0. "bigip_hash2 $bigip_hash2"}
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:$HTTP_HOST, URI:$HTTP_URI, VIP:[virtual name], MESG:$bigip_client_ip candidate hash2: $temp -> $bigip_hash2"}
if { [string compare $bigip_hash $client_hash]==0 or [string compare $bigip_hash2 $client_hash]==0 } {
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:$HTTP_HOST, URI:$HTTP_URI, VIP:[virtual name], MESG:$bigip_client_ip Valid request $uri_request"}
}
else {
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0. "$bigip_client_ip Invalid request $uri_request"}
log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:$HTTP_HOST, URI:$HTTP_URI, VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Invalid request $uri_request"
HTTP::respond 404 content "Invalid request"

}
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-cookies-enc-mergers {
when HTTP_RESPONSE {
set cookie_names [HTTP::cookie names]
foreach CookieName $cookie_names {
        if { [matchclass cookies_to_encrypt equals $CookieName] } { 
        HTTP::cookie encrypt "$CookieName" "8Te4RuD2asPa5REr85redRuV4VUqUxAb"
}
}
}


when HTTP_REQUEST {
set cookie_names [HTTP::cookie names]
foreach CookieName $cookie_names {
        if { [matchclass cookies_to_encrypt equals $CookieName] } { 
        HTTP::cookie decrypt "$CookieName" "8Te4RuD2asPa5REr85redRuV4VUqUxAb"
}
}
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-cookies-secureflag {
when HTTP_RESPONSE {
   if {[HTTP::header exists "Set-Cookie"]}{  
        set count 0   
         foreach aheader [HTTP::header values "Set-Cookie"] { 

                # Removes headers on the first iteration of the loop
                # This way cookie headers are not doubled up
                        if {$count equals 0}
                        {
                                HTTP::header remove "Set-Cookie" 
                                incr {count}
                        }

                        # The following statements set cookies based on the attributes
                        # that are already present or lacking..... 

                        if {not(([string tolower $aheader] contains "; secure") || ([string tolower $aheader] contains ";secure"))} {
                                HTTP::header insert Set-Cookie "$aheader; secure"
                        } else {
                                HTTP::header insert Set-Cookie "$aheader"

                        }
      }
   }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-force-https-forauth {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
  if { [HTTP::uri] contains "/authenticated/" } {
     HTTP::redirect https:\/\/[getfield [HTTP::host] ":" 1][HTTP::uri]
         log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Redirected"
  }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-headers-remove {
when RULE_INIT {
        # Create a list of the response headers to delete.  
        set static::headers_to_delete [list x-fdsa-node x-fdsa-pid x-fdsa-stats-ttfbw \
x-powered-by x-aspnet-version server factset-redirector-cluster-affinity \
        factset-redirector-host factset-redirector-thread fds-node fds-pid fds-stats-ttfbw
        ]

        # Log debug messages to /var/log/ltm?  1=yes, 0=no.
        set static::clocking_debug 0
}

when HTTP_REQUEST {
  set HTTP_URI [HTTP::uri]
  set HTTP_HOST [HTTP::host]
}

when HTTP_RESPONSE {
        # Remove all headers in the delete list
        foreach aHeader [HTTP::header names] {
                if {[matchclass $static::headers_to_delete equals [string tolower $aHeader]]}{
                        while {[HTTP::header exists $aHeader]}{
                           if {$static::clocking_debug} {
                                log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:$HTTP_HOST, URI:$HTTP_URI, VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Removing $aHeader: [HTTP::header value $aHeader]"
                        }
                                HTTP::header remove $aHeader
                        }
                }
        }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-insert-tls-cipher {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
        HTTP::header insert X-TLS-Protocol [SSL::cipher version]
     }
}
ltm rule /Common/http-method-whitelist {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    if { ! ( [class match [string toupper [HTTP::method]] equals valid_http_methods] ) } {
        log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Bad HTTP Method: [HTTP::method]"
        HTTP::respond 405
        reject
        event disable
    }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-method-whitelist-cauth {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    if { ! ( [class match [string toupper [HTTP::method]] equals valid_http_methods_cauth] ) } {
        log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Bad HTTP Method: [HTTP::method]"
        HTTP::respond 405
        reject
        event disable
    }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-mtls-client-cert-insert {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
  if {[SSL::cert 0] ne ""}{
    set tmpcn [X509::subject [SSL::cert 0]]
    set cn [findstr $tmpcn "CN=" 3]
    HTTP::header replace X-Client-Certificate-SAN $cn
    #HTTP::header insert X-Client-Certificate-Cer $tmpcn
    HTTP::header insert X-Client-Cert [b64encode [SSL::cert 0]]

  } else {
    HTTP::header remove X-Client-Certificate-SAN
  }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/http-protocol-header-insert {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
  if { [TCP::local_port] == "80" } {
    HTTP::header insert Protocol http
  } elseif { [TCP::local_port] == "443" } {
    HTTP::header insert Protocol https
  }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/log_http_headers_rule {
when CLIENT_ACCEPTED {
    set clientAccept 0
    set Httpreq 0
    set hsl [HSL::open -publisher /Common/publisher-remote-syslog]
    set CONNECTION_RECEIVE [clock clicks -milliseconds]
    set clientAccept 1
    #HSL::send $hsl "[IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port]"

}
when HTTP_REQUEST {
   set HTTP_REQUEST_RECEIVE [clock clicks -milliseconds]
   set myHost [HTTP::host]
   set myPath [HTTP::path]
   set myMethod [HTTP::method]
   #HSL::send $hsl "[IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port]"
   if {$clientAccept == 1 && $Httpreq == 0} { set Httpreq 1 }
   else
   { set clientAccept 0 }
   #HSL::send $hsl "[IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port]"

}
when HTTP_RESPONSE {
   set HTTP_RESPONSE_RECEIVE [expr {[clock clicks -milliseconds] - $HTTP_REQUEST_RECEIVE }]
   set CONNECTION_RESPONSE_RECEIVE [expr {[clock clicks -milliseconds] - $CONNECTION_RECEIVE}]
   set myConnect [HTTP::header Connection]
   set myStatus [HTTP::status]
   if {$clientAccept == 1}{HSL::send $hsl "[IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port] [IP::server_addr]:[TCP::server_port] $myMethod $myPath \"[clock format [clock seconds] -format "%a, %d %h %Y %T"]\" $myHost $HTTP_RESPONSE_RECEIVE  total_time $CONNECTION_RESPONSE_RECEIVE $myConnect $myStatus"}
   else {HSL::send $hsl "[IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port] [IP::server_addr]:[TCP::server_port] $myMethod $myPath \"[clock format [clock seconds] -format "%a, %d %h %Y %T"]\" $myHost $HTTP_RESPONSE_RECEIVE total_time 0  $myConnect $myStatus"}}
}

ltm rule /Common/rtsp-callstreet-audiotoken {
when RULE_INIT {
   # Log debug messages to /var/log/ltm?  1=yes, 0=no.
   set static::audiotoken_debug 0
}

when RTSP_REQUEST {

if {$static::audiotoken_debug} { log local0. "[RTSP::uri]"    }

set bigip_client_ip  [IP::client_addr]
set RTSP_METHOD [RTSP::method]
set uri_request [RTSP::uri]

# if RTSP method is SETUP or OPTIONS, let it thru without auth
if { $RTSP_METHOD == "SETUP"} {
   if {$static::audiotoken_debug} {log local0. "$bigip_client_ip method $RTSP_METHOD, done"}
   return
}
if { $RTSP_METHOD == "OPTIONS"} {
   if {$static::audiotoken_debug} {log local0. "$bigip_client_ip method $RTSP_METHOD, done"}
   return
}

set Filename [URI::basename $uri_request]
set client_hash [URI::query $uri_request auth]

set datenow [clock scan now]
set day_of_year_str [clock format $datenow -format %j]
scan $day_of_year_str "%d" day_of_year_int
set year [clock format  $datenow -format %Y]
#log local0. "day_of_year $day_of_year_int"
#log local0. "year $year"

if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0. "$bigip_client_ip sent hash $client_hash"}

set temp "$day_of_year_int$year,$Filename,$bigip_client_ip,secret"

#log local0. "Building hash from $temp"

set temp1 [b64encode $temp]
#log local0. "b64encoded $temp1"
set bigip_hash [b64encode [md5 $temp1]]
#log local0. "bigip_hash $bigip_hash"
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0.  "$bigip_client_ip candidate hash1: $temp -> $bigip_hash"}
set day_of_year_min_one {expr $day_of_year_int-1}
#log local0. "day_of_year_min_one $day_of_year_min_one"
set temp "$day_of_year_min_one$year,$Filename,$bigip_client_ip,secret"

#log local0. "constructed string2 $temp"

set temp1 [b64encode $temp]
#log local0. "b64encoded $temp1"
set bigip_hash2 [b64encode [md5 $temp1]]
#log local0. "bigip_hash2 $bigip_hash2"
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0.  "$bigip_client_ip candidate hash2: $temp -> $bigip_hash2"}

if { [string compare $bigip_hash $client_hash]==0 or [string compare $bigip_hash2 $client_hash]==0 } {
if {$static::audiotoken_http_debug} {log local0. "$bigip_client_ip Valid request $uri_request"}
}
else {
log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:, URI:[RTSP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Invalid request $RTSP_METHOD $uri_request"

RTSP::respond 404 BadToken "x-header\r\n\r\n  Hey, you need a token"

}
}
}
ltm rule /Common/rule-http-response-remove-keepalive {
#https://cdn.f5.com/product/bugtracker/ID714372.html
when HTTP_RESPONSE_RELEASE {
    HTTP::header remove keep-alive
}
}
ltm rule /Common/rule-http-version-identifier {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
  if { [HTTP2::active] } {
    HTTP::header insert X-http-ver h2
  } else {
    HTTP::header insert X-http-ver h1
  }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/rule-http-xfp-header-insert {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
  if { [TCP::local_port] == "80" } {
    HTTP::header insert X-Forwarded-Proto http
  } elseif { [TCP::local_port] == "443" } {
    HTTP::header insert X-Forwarded-Proto https
  }
}
}
ltm rule /Common/windows-uri-filter {
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    if { [HTTP::uri] contains "\/\." } {
        log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Contains dot"
        # HTTP::respond 200 "Connection" "close" "Blocked" "true"
        # TCP::close
    }

    switch -glob [string tolower [HTTP::uri]] {
        *cmd.exe* -
        *telnet.exe* -
        *root.exe* -
        *ping.exe* -
        *awstats.pl?* {
        log local0. "S_IP:[IP::client_addr], S_PORT:[TCP::client_port], D_IP:[IP::local_addr], D_PORT:[TCP::local_port], HOST:[HTTP::host], URI:[HTTP::uri], VIP:[virtual name], MESG:Bad URI attempted"
        HTTP::respond 405
        discard
        }
    }
}
}

    cipher ECDHE+AES-GCM:RSA+AES-GCM:-ADH:-EXP:-SSLv3:-TLSv1:-TLSv1_1:TLSv1_3:@STRENGTH
    dh-groups DEFAULT
    signature-algorithms DEFAULT
}

    authenticate once
    authenticate-depth 9

    cert /Common/auth.uat.factset.com_2024
    cert-key-chain {
        wildcard.uat.factset_THAWTE-INTERMEDIATE-RSA-CA_0 {
            cert /Common/auth.uat.factset.com_2024
            chain /Common/THAWTE-INTERMEDIATE-RSA-CA.crt
            key ******
        }
    }
    cipher-group /Common/FACTSET-CUSTOM-CIPHER-GROUP
    ciphers none
    defaults-from /Common/clientssl
    inherit-ca-certkeychain true
    inherit-certkeychain false
    key ******
    ocsp-stapling enabled
    options { dont-insert-empty-fragments no-tlsv1.1 no-sslv3 no-tlsv1 }
    peer-cert-mode require
    retain-certificate true
}

%DOSL7.captcha.solution%
